dropdown behavior when it is touched vs clicked.\n        // channels will be clickable on second click. first click simply opens the menu.\n        $('#channel-navigation > .sw-channel-item > a').on({\n            'touchstart': function (e) {\n                \n                // see if has menu\n                if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown li').length > 0) {\n                    var button = $(this);\n\n                    // add href as property if not already set\n                    // then remove href attribute\n                    if (!button.prop('linkHref')) {\n                        button.prop('linkHref', button.attr('href'));\n                        button.removeAttr('href');\n                    }\n\n                    // check to see if menu is already open\n                    if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown').is(':visible')) {\n                        // if open go to link\n                        window.location.href = button.prop('linkHref');\n                    } \n\n                } \n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n\n    \n    function channelHoverIE(){\n\t\t// set z-index for IE7\n\t\tvar parentZindex =       $(\".sw-channel-dropdown\").hide();\n\t        $(this).removeClass(\"hover\");\n\t        var subList = $(this).children('ul');\n\t        if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n\t            subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"true\");\n\t        }\n\t    });\n    }\n\n    function closeMenuByPressingKey() {\n        $(\".sw-channel-item\").each(function(ind) {\n            $(this).keyup(function (event) {\n                if (event.keyCode == 27) { // ESC\n                    $(\".sw-channel-dropdown\").hide();\n                    $(this).removeClass(\"hover\");\n                    var subList = $(this).children('ul');\n                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n                        subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"true\");\n                    }\n                    $(this).next().find('a:first').focus();\n                }\n            });\n        });\n\n        $(\".sw-channel-dropdown li\").each(function(ind) {\n community, believing that the rich cultures and languages of our students and families are not only an asset, but also an integral part of our shared identity and experience. As the Highline Community, we share in the commitment to engage in respectful, productive, and bipartisan civic engagement and communication in a safe and inclusive space.</div><div>&nbsp;</div><div>Highline is committed to ensuring that our students feel safe, welcomed and respected at school. This means we will continue to intervene when we see or hear offensive, bigoted words and actions. We are committed to our promise of knowing each of our students by name, strength and need, as well as protecting, advocating for and valuing our students equally no matter their race, language or ethnicity. To support this work, our School Board recently passed the attached Resolution in support of serving each of our students in an equitable and inclusive environment.</div><div>&nbsp;</div><div>Highline
